「It’s well known to those in the know that medicinal herbs can be found around this area. Now, let’s move ahead.」

With Elmefiora leading the way, we decide to go ahead.

I see, she must be a member of some high-ranking adventurer party. And they used to come here often. And then, for some reason, she left the party and is now looking for medicinal herbs.

「Wait, these ones are tough enemies. But the medicinal herbs are up ahead. Looks like we have no choice but to defeat them.」

After walking for a while, we find sheep-like monsters blocking our path.

They have two faces, thick legs, and long white fur. Not good, there are two of them.

Appraisal!

Two-headed Bristly Magic Goat, Rank 45

「They don’t seem to be a superior species. Rank 45. Be careful, one of them is going to cast two magic at the same time.」

「…」

It seems that Elmefiora has used Appraisal on them. She then starts to circulate her magical energy. She’s probably going to use magic.

Still, if even a rank 45 monster isn’t a superior species, as expected, this forest is too dangerous. And then, even if you have confidence in your skills, I’d say taking on two such high-ranked monsters at once isn’t something a sane person would do. Whatever her circumstances may be, she must really want to get her hands on the medicinal herbs.

「Elmefiora, wouldn’t it be better to retreat? As expected, it’s dangerous.」

Frederie, the leader, also suggests retreating. Since this powerful man says so, I think it would be better to follow his suggestion, but…

「It’s okay, those monsters are weak to fire. I’ll weaken them with magic, so I’m leaving the finishing blow to you guys.」

「… I see, but if we think we’re in an unfavorable position, we’ll take the liberty to retreat.」

It seems a battle is unavoidable.

As Frederie signals to his comrades, they split into two groups of two and move to the left and right. It seems they have no intention of protecting Elmefiora.

What should I do? While preparing to attack, it would probably be best to focus on protecting her with a shield. They don’t seem to be expecting me to join the battle, after all.

I take out a mithril shield from my storage and start to channel magical energy into it.

The moment the two goats start to circulate their magical energy, perhaps sensing that, Frederie and the others split to the left and right and move around them. It seems they are intending to surround the monster from the sides and behind.

I thought things would get dangerous for us, but they, who are moving speedily, are attracting the hate of the goats, so we might be safe to some extent.

「Please… o spirit of fire…」

Elmefiora mutters something under her breath as she activates her magic.

Ugh, what’s that? Sensing magical energy, I look up into the sky and see two spears of flame floating in the air.

It must be hard to create two spears of flames at the same time, but can you even hit moving targets with them? I think it would require a considerable level of magical energy manipulation, but surely…

The spears of flame are fired towards the monsters. Amazing, despite the fact that they’re some distance away, they hit the monsters perfectly, and the monsters are engulfed in flames and let out cries.

Ugh, that’s one ridiculously powerful magic. The hot wind reaches even us here. It seems Frederie and the others are also avoiding the heat and can’t get close to the monsters.

「「Baaaaaaaaaaa!」」

The goats let out cries and fire their magic at us.

Ugh, this, earth bullet and water cannon, it seems. Not good.

「Lower your head, Elmefiora!」

I step forward with my mithril shield and crouch down while protecting her.

A strong impact hit the mithril shield, but if I focus on defense, it’s no problem whatsoever.

「Tch.」

「Guah.」

「Damn it.」

「Ouch.」

The goats continue to relentlessly fire earth and water magic in all directions, including towards Frederie and the others.

One of them is using two magic at the same time, but the attacks are spread, so we should be able to withstand it somehow. But could we close in on such enemies?

「Let’s put off healing for later, let’s go!」

At Frederie’s signal, the four of them swiftly close in on the monsters and start unleashing attacks at them.

What incredible teamwork. As they slash at the goats from the side and back with their swords, the goats change position and fight back with their horns, but by that time Frederie and the others have already moved to the back and side of the goat, and the attack is turning one-sided. Magic must be hard to use at close range.

Even if the goats use magic, Frederie and the others are constantly on the move as they fight so that the monsters can’t lock on their target, so the probability of them getting hit seems low.

「Baaaaaaaa!」

Letting out death throes, one of the goats falls with a thud.

Alright, just a bit more. The other one is also covered in wounds and seems to be on the verge of death, so the battle is pretty much settled; the moment I think that, the goat charges in our direction.

Geeh?! What should I do? If it were just me, I could just dodge it, but I have Elmefiora behind me. I can’t dodge, and I don’t have time to hesitate. I probably won’t be able to stop that charge with a shield.

I quickly take out my mithril sledgehammer and channel magical energy into it. The speed of its charge isn’t that fast. I’ll match the timing and hit it.

Putting my shield down, I throw the sledgehammer, which I’m holding with both hands, with a right swing at the goat, which is charging at me with its feet stomping on the ground.

「Take that!」

With a heavy thud, my swing cleanly hits the left side of the goat.

I did it… huh…

「Guaaaaaah!」

Driven by its momentum, the goat crashes into me just like that. It has two heads, so one of them hits me in the stomach.

Crap, damn it, I get sent flying backwards.

The damage is… none. It seems, thanks to my armor, I suffered no injuries, and was just knocked backwards.

「Sei-kun, are you okay?」

Elmefiora comes running towards me.

Damn it, I ended up showing her my useless side.

No, that’s not it. If it was the usual me, I should have been able to fight better.

More importantly, the goat.

「The monster?」

「Yes, as you can see over there.」

When I look in the direction Elmefiora is pointing, I see the goat lying on the ground, not moving at all. It seems to be dead.

「Phweeee~, you’re not half bad, Sei. It might be wounded, but to think you would to defeat that monster.」

The good-natured Brai praises me.

I see, it seems the monster died from my full-power blow.

The reason I was blown away was probably because I couldn’t also kill the momentum of its charge with my sledgehammer attack.

「Still, for you to have a mithril shield and sledgehammer, looks like you’re no ordinary porter.」

Frederie continues to glare at me.

Tch, this man, somehow, I think I should never let my guard down around him.

The other three seem friendly and have good personalities, but Frederie alone seems like he will never open up to me.

At any rate, I throw the monsters’ corpses into my storage. I can just dismantle them later.

「Hoh~, to think you’re able to put monsters that big into your storage.」

「「「…」」」

Everyone is silent, but with this, they must have realized that I am no ordinary person.

With this, I hope they won’t entertain any funny thoughts when night comes, but…

「Let’s hurry up. It’s just ahead.」

Once we finish recovering, we start walking after Elmefiora.

+++

# **179 - To the Demonic Dragon Mountain Range 2**

「It’s up ahead.」

With Elmefiora leading the way, we keep walking for a while and reach an open area. It looks like a grassland. There’s vegetation about 50cm high.

「Be careful, not only high-ranked rabbits but also monsters from the sky will attack you here.」

「So, what should we do?」

「I want you to defeat any monsters that come near while I collect the medicinal herbs. You don’t have to kill them, it’s enough as long as you can buy me some time.」

「「「…」」」

We fall into silence as we listen to Frederie and Elmefiora’s conversation.

In the grassland spreading out in front of us, the grass and trees are swaying gently in the wind, but there’s an indescribable eerie atmosphere in the air. Most likely, a powerful monster is lurking there.

Drat, I have a bad feeling about this and I can’t stop sweating. It’s a bit too dangerous, isn’t it? But thinking about Elmefiora, I can’t afford to back down there.

「Sei, you take up your shield and protect Elmefiora. We’ll surround you on all sides and fight to keep the enemies away.」

「Yeah…」

If Frederie and the others are going to protect me and Elmefiora, then there’s nothing more reassuring. There’s no room for doubt about their abilities.

「However, if I judge that we won’t be able to protect you, we’ll take the liberty to retreat. The job we accepted is to accompany you gather medicinal herbs, not to serve as your guards, after all.」

「Yeah, that’s fine.」

Geeh, seriously?

I see, so that’s why they didn’t protect Elmefiora in the battle against the goats. Damn it, it looks like I can’t rely on them completely. I’ll also have to be constantly on the alert and take part in the battle. If possible, I would rather wait here, though.

「Umm, Sei-kun, you’re a porter, so you don’t have to push yourself. You can wait here…」

「No need to worry. I’ve been to the demonic dragon mountain range many times, after all. I’ll definitely protect you, Elmefiora-san.」

「Sei-kun…」

Shoot, I end up getting carried away.

However, staying here alone is similarly dangerous. In that case, the best thing to do here is to act cool and do her a favor. Besides, maybe I’m just worrying too much. There’s also the chance that we’ll be able to collect the medicinal herbs surprisingly easily.

「Alright, are you ready? Everyone, crouch. There might be a monster that’s good at detecting magical energy. As much as possible, we’ll go at it without using magic until we get into battle.」

Frederie and the others unsheathe their red iron swords and start to move while maintaining their combat readiness.

I see, I guess mithril equipment is disadvantageous in a situation like this. When you channel magical energy into mithril equipment, its attack and defense power increases, but when you don’t channel magical energy into it, it is incredibly fragile. That’s probably why most adventurers wear red iron equipment. Well, I’m a porter and can keep all sorts of equipment in my storage, so if I can use it well, I think I’ll be fine.

I take out an iron shield and stand close to Elmefiora.

「…」

Everyone is silent as we step into the grassland, concealing our presence all the while.

Not good, I’m crazy nervous.

I start walking while making full use of my presence detection and magical energy perception skills. I don’t think there are any presence of enemies nearby, but I can’t let my guard down. There may be a type of monster that can hide their presence. Besides, I feel like there’s a powerful monster somewhere. Well, they’re probably everywhere in this forest, so it’s only natural that there are, though.

「…」

We keep walking for a while, but we still haven’t encountered any enemies. However, Elmefiora is unable to find any medicinal herbs, so we have no choice but to continue further in.

Everyone is silent, but their steps are slowing down. They probably don’t want to go any further.

「Elmefiora, any further is…」

「Ah, there it is, yellow silk grass.」

Just as Frederie stops walking and decides to retreat, Elmefiora seems to have found the medicinal herb.

The moment everyone relaxes their mind in relief, Jocon on the left releases his magical energy and leaps out.

Clang!

A metallic sound rings out, and when I look over, I see Jocon exchanging blows with a monster with his sword.

Appraisal!

Head-hunting Vorpal Rabbit, Rank 41

It’s a large rabbit, about two meters long, with sharp claws extending from its hands, and it is calm as it blocks Jocon’s red iron sword. Its slanted red eyes are radiating murderous intent, and although I can’t read its expression, it appears to be angry. I wonder if it identified us as foreign enemies invading its territory.

Clang, clang, clang!

「Kuh, this guy, it’s fast!」

Jocon and the rabbit are exchanging blows, but he can do nothing but defend himself against the rabbit’s series of attacks. Not good, it’s an agility-type monster, which I’m not good against.

「Haaah!」

Rogyra joins the fight from the side, closing in on the rabbit at high speed with instant step and unleashing a sideways slash at it.

A red horizontal slash runs across the rabbit’s stomach, causing it to bleed. He then unleashes a follow-up thrust attack, but the rabbit escapes to its rear with a swift movement.

「Alright, just like this, let’s retreat…」

「Not yet, I haven’t gotten enough medicinal herbs yet.」

「But…」

「Please, just a bit more, I only need a bit more, so…」

「Tch, other monsters might come over. Hurry up.」

Frederie is about to decide to retreat, but it seems we haven’t gotten enough medicinal herbs yet. This is yellow silk grass, huh. I guess I’ll look for it, too.

Jocon and Rogyra start fighting the rabbit, making a violent metallic sound echo through the area. With such a fierce battle, the monsters nearby should have noticed our presence, too. It should be fine if I use my magical energy too.

I put the iron shield into my storage, take out a mithril shield, and channel some magical energy into it.

「Damn it, looks like there’s another one in the back, Brai, I’ll join the battle too. Whether to serve as their guard or retreat, you can act according to your own judgement.」

「Roger.」

Fredeire also goes off towards the rabbits.

As before, Elmefiora is desperately searching around for medicinal herbs. I also try to look for them while keeping an eye on the surrounding area, but I just can’t seem to find them.

Buzzzzzzz.

Not good, this buzzing sound. I have a bad feeling about this.

「Elmefiora, Sei, get ready to retreat.」

When I hear Brai’s voice, I look into the sky, to see a swarm of mad bees beginning to circle around there.

Appraisal!

Mad Bee, Rank 33

Not only is their rank high, there are too many of them. It’s not realistic to fight them.

I start to channel magical energy into my shield. It’s time to retreat.

「Ah, there it is, over there!」

Elmefiora seems to have found the medicinal herb.

The direction she is pointing is directly below where the bees are circling around. Are you serious? As expected, I don’t have the guts to go there.

「No, let go!」

「No can do, we have to retreat.」

Brai grabs Elmefiora, who is trying to head towards the medicinal herbs, and is trying to retreat.

That’s a natural decision. We can just come here again after some time, after all.

「Please, I don’t have much time. Let go!」

「…」

Elmefiora refuses to back down.

As expected, it seems like she has some kind of situation.

Damn it, it’s too dangerous to stay here like this. And I absolutely don’t want to come back here again.

I take out one strength restorative medicine from my storage and throw it into my mouth. If it’s just me, I should be able to manage one way or another, even if I take some damage.

「Sei!」

「Sei-kun!」

With the voices of the two behind me, I use instant step and jump out directly under the swarm of bees.

The yellow silk grass is…over there.

As soon as I catch sight of the medicinal herb I’m after, I feel the swarm of bees closing in.

No good, I won’t make it in time. The attack is coming!

「Oraaa!」

Bashing them with my magical energy-imbued mithril shield, I knock down the approaching bees and push my way forward, toying with them with zigzag movements so they can’t lock their target on me.

I got it! I skillfully slip through the bees’ attacks and pull out the yellow silk grass I am after from the ground. There is another one nearby, so I take it too. With this many, it should be enough…

「Ugh.」

Thud thud thud.

I feel an impact on my back.

Damn it, it seems I’ve been hit by the bees’ stinger attacks.

Two of them hit me through my armor so they don’t do any damage, but one is aimed at the gap in my armor and causes me excruciating pain.

I crush the strength restorative medicine in my mouth and swallow it. Then, swinging my shield around, I start running in the direction of Elmefiora and Brai.

「I got the yellow silk grass. Run!」

Urged by Brai, Elmefiora begins to run back the way we came.

It seems Frederie and the others have also decided to retreat.

I continue running while serving as the rear guard. The dreadful buzzing of bees is echoing behind me. Holy shit, just how many of them are there? If I group up with my comrades now, I’ll end up taking these bees with me. But staying here is not an option.

At that moment, I sense a tremendous amount of magical energy in the sky above me.

This, is it Elmefiora’s magic? If so, I can be at ease…

Slash! Slash slash! Slash slash slash slash slash slash slash slash!

Blades of wind with tremendous firepower are generated, chopping up the bees one after the other.

Yay, with this, I’m saved.

Slash slash slash slash slash slash slash slash!

「Ouch!」

The blades of wind rain down on me, too.

Elmefiora-san, to think you’d attack me as well… W, well, it’s an emergency, so I guess it can’t be helped. The demonic dragon armor I’m wearing gives me wind magic resistance, so it’s not that big of a deal, though.

Still, that’s incredibly powerful wind magic. Err, it has that much firepower, so if I wasn’t wearing armor with wind resistance, I might have ended up on the verge of death, you know?

Buzzzzzzzzzzzzzz!

「Huh?」

Along with a loud buzzing sound, I sense powerful magical energy in the sky above and look up.

There, I see a giant dragonfly hovering in the air, unleashing wind magic and mowing down the bees one after another.

Appraisal!

Six-winged Gluttonous Demon Dragonfly, Rank 77

「Geehh?!」

Crap, I’m going to die.

So the user of wind magic is not Elmefiora, but this dragonfly, huh.

What should I do? Fighting is not an option. I have no choice but to run away.

I hide my presence and blend in with the bee corpses so as not to attract its attention. Then, without looking back, I slowly move towards Elmefiora and the others.

「…」

It’ll be fine, right? Well, even if it fires wind magic at me, my armor should be able to withstand it. What to do if it uses earth magic or something… At any rate, there’s no point in thinking about that. Erasing my sound and presence, I somehow manage to get out of the grassland and return alive to where Elmefiora is.

When I look back for one last time, I see the dragonfly munching on the bee it has killed. I feel like our eyes meet, but it seems to be engrossed in its meal and shows no signs of attacking us.

「Sei, you did well make it out alive.」

「Sei-kun, thank you so much.」

「Well, this much is nothing. More importantly, let’s hurry on.」

The truth is, thinking that I was going to die, I was so close to peeing my pants, but I can’t help but act cool in front of a beautiful woman.

At any rate, we’ve managed to find the yellow silk grass safely. All that’s left is the propagating magic moss and the magic polypore.

We start walking towards the next medicinal herb gathering spot.

+++

# **180 - To the Demonic Dragon Mountain Range 3**

「Sei, you did well make it out alive.」

As we finally move away from the grassland and take a breather, erasing our noise all the while, Brai speaks to me.

I was really lucky. Not only was I lucky that I was wearing armor that resisted wind magic, I was also saved by the fact that the dragonfly was busy preying upon the bees and didn’t chase me.

「Sei-kun, um, you really saved me there. Thanks to you, I was able to get the medicinal herbs safely.」

「Well, my body just moved on its own.」

Alright, it’s worth taking the risk. This Elmefiora, she must be very grateful to me. However, I must refrain from selling favors so blatantly.

Elmefiora is very beautiful and has a nice figure, so she has been getting sexual gazes from men, and there’s the possibility that she’s fed up with that. Perhaps that’s also why she is hiding her face. I’m different from other men and have no funny ulterior motives; let’s interact with her in such a manner. Yes, unable to just leave alone the admirable Elmefiora who is gathering medicinal herbs due to some kind of circumstances, I support her selflessly, without regard for the danger; let’s go with that. Even if frontal attack is impossible, with this method, the possibility of deepening my relationship with her in the future must have sprouted, even if only slightly.

After that, we make our way through the forest with Elmefiora taking the lead, taking a break in between and fighting monsters a number of times.

「I want to gather one more medicinal herb today. Once that’s done, let’s prepare for the night camp.」

Phew, looks like once we gather the next medicinal herb, we’ll be done for today. I narrowly escaped death earlier, so I’ll stay put next time.

「And, you see, about the next medicinal herb, it’s located in a place that’s very difficult for me to gather…」

It’s difficult for Elmefiora to gather, I wonder if it’s on a rock wall or something of the sort. Somehow, I’m starting to have a really bad feeling about this.

「The magic polypore grows on the trunk of a high-ranked demon tree. Moreover, it’s pretty high up.」

「「「…」」」

Everyone falls silent.

What the, for it to grow on a monster of all places. How on earth are we going to pick it?

「Which means we’re going to defeat that demon tree?」

「No, it’s impossible to defeat that monster. You have to erase your presence, close in on it and cut off the medicinal herb in one go. Then retreat right away. It’s located in a place I can’t reach, so I’d like to ask someone to do with it for me…」

「I see. In any case, I can’t make a judgement without seeing it. Lead the way.」

I listen to Frederie and Elmefiora’s conversation, and somehow it sounds legit dangerous.

A monster that Elmefiora and the Rhapsody members can’t defeat, the heck is that. It must be a fairly high-ranked monster, but I wonder if Frederie and the others will actually harvest the medicinal herbs without regard for the danger. They have no reason to risk their lives, so it looks like the task of collecting the medicinal herb will fall on me, but… in any case, as Frederie says, we won’t get anywhere without seeing it.

Under the guidance of Elmefiora, we make our way through the forest.

「That one.」

「…」

Further into the forest, where there is strangely no presence of monsters at all, stands a giant tree. Its height… I can’t tell exactly, but it must be over a hundred meters. That’s the old demon tree we’re looking for, huh.

Looking more closely, there are fan-shaped mushrooms dotted around the trunk of the giant tree. Even the ones closest to the base of the three are probably around ten meters high. They’re in a place that you can’t reach, although not absolutely, without using body enhancement.

「Those are the magic polypore. Can someone go and collect them?」

「「「…」」」

Everyone falls silent.

It’s that huge of a monster. Its rank should be pretty high too, so it’s just too dangerous.

As expected, even I end up getting cold feet. However, Elmefiora might have some ingenious ideas. She knows there are medicinal herbs here, and she should know how to pick them. Depending on the plan, perhaps I won’t mind going and picking them.

「… It can’t be helped. I’ll go and pick them.」

Huh, seriously? As expected, it’s too much for Elmefiora, a magician, isn’t it?

Elmefiora seems to have made up her mind. From her gaze, I can see her determination to go and pick them no matter what. I don’t know her situation, but she seems to be in a very desperate situation. I’d like to help her if I can.

「Wait, I’ll go.」

「Huh, Sei-kun?」

「I can use presence concealment skill, and I have all kinds of weapons and tools in my storage. Elmefiora-san, tell me more about that old demon tree.」

「Yes, umm, that would be a great help. You can decide whether to actually go or not after hearing what I share with you.」

Having come this far, as expected, I can’t say I’m quitting since it’s too dangerous. That’ll bring shame upon myself as a man.

At any rate, let’s gather information and find the best way to tackle it.

「You see, that old demon tree not only uses earth, wind, water, and shadow magic, but also attacks using its roots, branches, and leaves.」

「I, I see…」

Geeh, that guy is just as dangerous as I thought. There seems to be no escape, up, down, left, right, or even in the air. It might even be stronger than a demonic dragon. Damn it, it makes me want to go home.

「But that monster, you know, sometimes doesn’t notice even if you give it a little bit of stimulation. Sometimes it will stretch out its branches and roots far away to attack, but sometimes it shows no reaction at all. Umm, you could say it’s all down to luck.」

What does that mean? Is it that when it’s hungry it preys on anything that comes close, and when it’s full it deliberately doesn’t attack its prey? Or is it simply a matter of mood?

In any case, there doesn’t seem to be any ingenious idea. While erasing your presence, you close in on it and collect the medicinal herbs in one breath, and then retreat right away; like that’s the only way.

The problem is the earth magic it uses. My armor is weak against earth magic, so if I get hit by earth magic unleashed by a high-ranked monster, I might really die. Since it’s a demon tree, it must have spread its roots across the area, so its attack range is probably large. What should I do?

「Sei-kun, if push comes to shove, I think I can use magic to interfere with earth and wind to block the monster’s attacks, but I can only do either earth or wind at a time.」

「I see, in that case, earth, please.」

「Yes, that would probably be better. I’ll do my best to block the monster’s earth magic and root attacks.」

This is good news. I don’t know how much Elmefiora can hold back the monster’s attacks, but the chances of me being hit by earth magic have decreased significantly. As things stand, it might go unexpectedly smoothly.

I steady my breath and take out a red iron sword from storage. So that I won’t get detected by the monster, I need to cut off the magic polypore without channeling any magical energy. How did I get my hands on this sword, again? I think it’s something I took from the beastfolk bandit band that Ottilie of the Cotton Clouds had defeated.

「Oh, that’s quite a sword.」

「…」

Frederie stares at me, as if licking me all over.

Damn it, what’s with that guy’s gaze? It’s as creepy as ever.

The others are silent, but they are staring at me curiously. Well, not only do I have physical abilities unthinkable from an ordinary porter, I’m clad in a full set of demonic dragon armor, I use a mithril sword and shield, and now, I’ve taken out a red iron sword of considerable purity. They’re probably curious about my true identity.

「Alright, let’s do it. Everyone, please wait here.」

While using presence concealment, I break into a run towards the old demon tree.

The surrounding area is completely silent. It’s as if there are no living creatures at all. I wonder if everything that comes close ends up getting preyed upon by it.

No matter how hard I try to muffle the noise, every time I step on fallen leaves or dead wood, some kind of sound comes out.

*Thump, thump* I can feel my heart beating loudly in my chest. It seems this guy sometimes shows no reaction to intruders, so please, ignore me.

It’s huge.

I reach a place about a few dozen meters away from the old demon tree. The trunk of the giant tree is incredibly huge, on a completely different level compared to the ones I have defeated before. I can understand why Elmefiora said we couldn’t defeat it.

I concentrate my mind and use my presence detection skill, but there’s no reaction in the surrounding area at all.

I’ve come this far. All that’s left is to close in on it and cut off the medicinal herbs with my sword in one breath.

What should I do? The magic polypores are in a location that can’t be reached from the ground. While using light body enhancement, putting my foot on the trunk, jumping, and cutting them off in one go should do it. As expected, it’ll probably notice me, but if I quickly retreat from this place, I should be able to manage one way or another. There’s also the possibility that nothing will happen unexpectedly. Yes, perhaps all of that is the so-called needless worry.

「Let’s do it.」

I look at the magic polypore growing on the trunk of a giant tree and hold my sword at the ready.

So as not to stimulate the monster, I’ll keep my body enhancement to the minimum. I’ll gently put my foot on the trunk and jump towards the medicinal herbs. Should I channel some magical energy into my sword when I cut them off? I don’t know how hard the medicinal herbs are, after all.

I steady my breath and prepare myself. Let’s do it, let’s go. I’m sure that when I finish collecting the medicinal herbs, Elmefiora will look at me with affection-filled eyes.

Thump, thump, thump… Let’s go.

I leap out towards the old demon tree. I kick the ground a few meters away from it and put my foot on the trunk.

Here it is. There is no room for failure. I put my foot on a slight protrusion on the trunk, jump towards a magic polypore, and swing my red iron sword down.

The magic polypore is semicircular and about one meter long. I sink the red iron sword into its base area, close to the trunk.

「Alright… huh?!」

Shoot, the magic polypore is surprisingly hard, and I cut through about 80% of it with my sword, but it won’t come off the trunk. What should I do, should I do it one more time? No, as expected, that’s not a good idea. The monster will definitely notice me. I can’t afford to miss this chance.

Whuoooooooo.

In addition to my body enhancement, I also channel magical energy into my red iron sword and swing it down in one go.

Slash!!

I, I did it. I successfully cut off the magic polypore.

Before I hit the ground, I put my sword and the medicinal herb into my storage. All that’s left to do is turn back the way I came in a straight line. I did it.

The moment I hit the ground.

Rumble rumble rumble rumble rumble.

「Geeeh?!」

The ground begins to shake violently, and at the same time, I sense an intense flow of magical energy from the surrounding area.

Not good, an attack is coming. At any rate, I’ve got to get out of here…

「Damn it.」

The ground shakes violently, and begins to crack.

Not good, I can’t brace my legs on the ground.

I sense strong magical energy from the ground. Not good, an attack is coming…

「Sei-kun, hurry up!」

At the same time as I hear Elmefiora’s voice from afar, the shaking of the ground stops.

To be precise, it’s shaking slightly, but it seems that Elmefiora is interfering with the ground and holding the monsters back.

I kick the ground using full-strength body enhancement and head towards Elmefiora and the others.

Alright, I can do it.

I succeed in getting away from the hold demon tree. Just like this, I’ll withdraw from the front line…

「Sei, above!!」

At the same time as Brai shouts, both my magical energy perception and presence detection pick up a reaction.

I instantly look up to the sky, and see a large branch of the old demon tree getting swung down towards me.

Not good, at this rate, I’ll get a direct hit.

I quickly escape to the side with instant step.

Booooooooom.

The branch of the old demon tree explodes into the ground. The sound of the impact that splits the ground echoes through the area, and a cloud of dust spread over the area.

Appraisal!

Ten Thousand Years Agarwood Great Demon Tree, Rank 108

… I’m at a loss for words. All I can do now is to withdraw from the front line.

Instant step!

I blend into the dust and jump out in one go.

Alright, I can do it, just a bit more and I’ll…

「Huh?」

I feel a strange sensation on my legs and end up losing my balance.

What’s going on? Elmefiora should have interfered with the ground…

「This is… shadow magic?!」

That old demon tree, noticing that it can’t use earth magic, it chooses to use shadow magic.

The shadow extending from the trunk of the giant tree is twining around my feet.

However, not only am I quite far away from the trunk, direct sunlight is shining on me, so the binding force shouldn’t be that high.

What should I do? Shall I shake it off by force, or with light magic…?

「Geeeh?!」

Sensing magical energy, I turn my eyes to the trunk, and see that suddenly two large water balls are getting created around it.

Not good, it’s water magic. What should I do? Damn it, first thing first, I need to prioritize my defense.

I give up on trying to undo the shadow magic, take out two mithril shields from my storage, and start to channel magical energy on them. More, I need to channel magical energy into them to the limit.

Whoooooosh!!

With the force of a flood, two powerful water cannons shoot out at me from the water balls.

「Guaaaaaaah!」

I block the magic with my shields, but the impact is so great that I end up getting blown away.

Shoot, my shield…

As the impact hits my whole body, I end up letting go of both of my shields, and my body gets knocked into the ground over and over again.

What should I do, should I heal myself first or run, not good, I’m going to die…

「Sei!」

Brai grabs my body and carries me away.

It seems that thanks to getting hit by the water magic, I have been blown far away towards my comrades.

My body… seems to be fine. I’m bruised all over my body, but my life is not in danger. At most, the wrists of both of my hands, which were holding the shields, are painful.

We somehow manage to get away from that place.

+++
